\u003cdiv class=\"visual-stat\"\u003e\n                            \u003cdiv class=\"stat-number\"\u003e2.5M+\u003c/div\u003e\n                            \u003cdiv class=\"stat-text\"\u003eHappy class=\"stat-number\"\u003e50K+\u003c/div\u003e\n                            \u003cdiv class=\"stat-text\"\u003eDaily Calculations\u003c/div\u003e\n                        \u003c/div\u003e\n                        \u003cdiv class=\"visual-stat\"\u003e\n                            \u003cdiv class=\"stat-number\"\u003e4.8★\u003c/div\u003e\n                            \u003cdiv class=\"stat-text\"\u003eAverage Rating\u003c/div\u003e\n                        \u003c/div\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/section\u003e\n\n    \u003c!-- FAQ Section --\u003e\n    \u003csection class=\"faq-section\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class=\"container\"\u003e\n            \u003cdiv class=\"section-header\"\u003e\n                \u003ch2 class=\"section-title\"\u003eFrequently Asked Questions\u003c/h2\u003e\n                \u003cp class=\"section-description\"\u003eEverything you need to know about BMI\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cdiv class=\"faq-container\"\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class=\"faq-item\"\u003e\n                    \u003cbutton class=\"faq-question\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"faq1\"\u003e\n                        \u003cspan\u003eWhat is BMI and why is it important?\u003c/span\u003e\n                        \u003csvg class=\"faq-icon\" width=\"24\" height=\"24\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\n                            \u003cpath d=\"M19 9L12 16L5 9\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\"/\u003e\n                        \u003c/svg\u003e\n                    \u003c/button\u003e\n                    \u003cdiv class=\"faq-answer\" id=\"faq1\"\u003e\n                        \u003cp\u003eBMI (Body Mass Index) is a measurement that uses your height and weight to estimate body fat. It's an important screening tool that helps identify potential health risks associated with being underweight, overweight, or obese. While BMI doesn't directly measure body fat, it's a useful indicator for most adults.\u003c/p\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class=\"faq-item\"\u003e\n                    \u003cbutton class=\"faq-question\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"faq2\"\u003e\n                        \u003cspan\u003eHow accurate is the BMI calculator?\u003c/span\u003e\n                        \u003csvg class=\"faq-icon\" width=\"24\" height=\"24\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\n                            \u003cpath d=\"M19 9L12 16L5 9\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\"/\u003e\n                        \u003c/svg\u003e\n                    \u003c/button\u003e\n                    \u003cdiv class=\"faq-answer\" id=\"faq2\"\u003e\n                        \u003cp\u003eOur BMI calculator uses the standard formula recognized by health organizations worldwide. However, BMI has limitations - it doesn't account for muscle mass, bone density, age, or gender. Athletes and very muscular individuals may have a high BMI without excess body fat. Always consult healthcare professionals for comprehensive health assessments.\u003c/p\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class=\"faq-item\"\u003e\n                    \u003cbutton class=\"faq-question\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"faq3\"\u003e\n                        \u003cspan\u003eWhat is a healthy BMI range?\u003c/span\u003e\n                        \u003csvg class=\"faq-icon\" width=\"24\" height=\"24\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\n                            \u003cpath d=\"M19 9L12 16L5 9\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\"/\u003e\n                        \u003c/svg\u003e\n                    \u003c/button\u003e\n                    \u003cdiv class=\"faq-answer\" id=\"faq3\"\u003e\n                        \u003cp\u003eAccording to the World Health Organization (WHO), a healthy BMI for adults ranges from 18.5 to 24.9. A BMI below 18.5 is considered underweight, 25.0-29.9 is overweight, and 30.0 or higher indicates obesity. These ranges apply to most adults but may vary for different populations and age groups.\u003c/p\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class=\"faq-item\"\u003e\n                    \u003cbutton class=\"faq-question\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"faq4\"\u003e\n                        \u003cspan\u003eCan I use BMI if I'm pregnant or breastfeeding?\u003c/span\u003e\n                        \u003csvg class=\"faq-icon\" width=\"24\" height=\"24\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\n                            \u003cpath d=\"M19 9L12 16L5 9\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\"/\u003e\n                        \u003c/svg\u003e\n                    \u003c/button\u003e\n                    \u003cdiv class=\"faq-answer\" id=\"faq4\"\u003e\n                        \u003cp\u003eBMI is not an accurate measure for pregnant or breastfeeding women, as it doesn't account for the natural and healthy weight gain during these periods. If you're pregnant or breastfeeding, please consult your healthcare provider for appropriate weight monitoring and health assessments.\u003c/p\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class=\"faq-item\"\u003e\n                    \u003cbutton class=\"faq-question\" aria-expanded=\"false\" aria-controls=\"faq5\"\u003e\n                        \u003cspan\u003eHow often should I check my BMI?\u003c/span\u003e\n                        \u003csvg class=\"faq-icon\" width=\"24\" height=\"24\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\n                            \u003cpath d=\"M19 9L12 16L5 9\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\"/\u003e\n                        \u003c/svg\u003e\n                    \u003c/button\u003e\n                    \u003cdiv class=\"faq-answer\" id=\"faq5\"\u003e\n                        \u003cp\u003eFor general health monitoring, checking your BMI once a month is sufficient. If you're actively working on weight management or following a fitness program, you might check more frequently. Remember that small fluctuations are normal, and long-term trends are more important than daily changes.\u003c/p\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/section\u003e\n\n    \u003c!-- Health Disclaimer --\u003e\n    \u003csection class=\"disclaimer-section\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class=\"container\"\u003e\n            \u003cdiv class=\"disclaimer-card\"\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class=\"disclaimer-icon\"\u003e\n                    \u003csvg width=\"24\" height=\"24\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\n                        \u003cpath d=\"M12 9V13M12 17H12.01M21 12C21 16.9706 16.9706 21 12 21C7.02944 21 3 16.9706 3 12C3 7.02944 7.02944 3 12 3C16.9706 3 21 7.02944 21 12Z\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\"/\u003e\n                    \u003c/svg\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class=\"disclaimer-content\"\u003e\n                    \u003ch3 class=\"disclaimer-title\"\u003eMedical Disclaimer\u003c/h3\u003e\n                    \u003cp class=\"disclaimer-text\"\u003eThis BMI calculator is for informational purposes only and does not constitute medical advice. BMI is a screening tool and has limitations. It doesn't directly measure body fat and may not be accurate for athletes, elderly individuals, or certain populations. Always consult with qualified healthcare professionals for personalized medical advice, diagnosis, or treatment. If you have concerns about your weight or health, please seek professional medical guidance.\u003c/p\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n
